# D.0.1 Gap Inventory + Corpus Manifest — Documentation Truth Campaign

**Sub-Phase D.0.1 deliverable** — read-only forensic sweep of the prose surfaces D.0 named but did not reach, plus the campaign's durable **corpus manifest**. Governing doc: [`CLAIMS_ARCHAEOLOGY_FRAMEWORK.md`](CLAIMS_ARCHAEOLOGY_FRAMEWORK.md). Companion to [`D0_CLAIMS_INVENTORY.md`](D0_CLAIMS_INVENTORY.md); same row format, states, and flags so the two merge cleanly. Records false/stale/unverifiable claims; corrects nothing.

| | |
|---|---|
| **Sweep date** | 2026-06-13 |
| **HEAD at sweep** | `9693649d8` (Fluids-Integration.F.1.4 FINAL) |
| **Method** | Job 1 manifest enumeration (git ls-files − journey/archive − D.0-swept) → Job 2 two-pass sweep of the 386-file gap set, fanned out across 29 groups + 1 gap-closer agent. Present-tense current-accuracy claims only; historical narration out of scope. |
| **Claims inventoried** | 873 present-tense claims across the 386-file gap set (388 coverage entries incl. 1 path variant, §7.2) |
| **Source modifications** | none (this report is the only file written) |

### 1.2 Manifest arithmetic (it balances)

| Set | Count |
|---|---:|
| Total tracked `.md` / `.markdown` (`git ls-files`) | 1,437 |
| − OUT-OF-SCOPE (`docs/journey/**` + `docs/archive/**`, by rule) | 913 |
| = **In-scope corpus** | **524** |
| · SWEPT-BY-D0 (D.0 §1.3) | 138 |
| · **SWEEP-NOW-D0.1** (this sub-phase) | **386** |

`138 + 386 = 524`. Every in-scope file is now accounted for; the leftover is zero. (Non-`.md` in-scope surfaces: `gh-pages/index.html` + `gh-pages/_config.yml` were swept by D.0; the remaining `gh-pages/` entries are images/CSS, not prose.)

### 1.3 Ground truth (carried from D.0 §1.2, re-anchored at HEAD)

Every VERIFIED/STALE row below is anchored on the D.0 §1.2 ground-truth table (130 members; ~39,900 test markers; fluids = 3 solvers with `UnifiedSolver` deleted + `ResearchFluidSystem` never a type; HNSW linear; SpatialHash dormant; phi3:medium default; WebSocket not QUIC; 8-stage deterministic ECS; toolchain 1.89.0; only `editor*` cargo aliases exist; hello_companion 7 modes) or on the agent's own grep at HEAD — never on another document.

## 3. Inventory (D.0.1)

One row per claim. States: VERIFIED / STALE / FABRICATED / UNVERIF (UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP) / ASPIR (ASPIRATIONAL-AS-PRESENT) / NEEDS-GLOBAL. Flags: 🟥 POISON-LIST · 🔧 CODE-FINDING · 📒 REGISTRY-CANDIDATE · ⚠️ CONTRADICTION (internal contradiction → D.1 reconcile-or-collapse, not patch).

### 4.3 Patterns

- **150 of the 386 files yielded zero present-tense claims** — pure historical narration (completion reports, session summaries, dated diagnostics, phase plans, `.zencoder/chats`, PBR `*_TASK*_COMPLETE`). They are read end-to-end and tagged in the manifest with `#Cl 0`; that is coverage proof, not a miss. The campaign's thesis holds: the corpus is mostly process-exhaust, and the live poison concentrates in a small set of "current-state" documents that nobody reconciled.
- **The render plans are the priority-1 confirmation.** `RENDERER_DEEP_ANALYSIS_AND_MEGALIGHTS_PLAN.md` and `RENDERER_MASTER_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md` assert `103k+ entity capacity @ 60 FPS` as a present-tense ✅ Strength (STALE — superseded by the 12,700-agents headline; and entity-iteration ≠ agent capacity) and restate `10.4× Unity / 2.1-5.2× Unreal` with **invented baseline counts** (Unity 9,900 / Unreal 20k-50k) — FABRICATED, no citable source. `COMPREHENSIVE_AUDIT_REPORT.md` carries the same 103k/370-FPS pair and is the single worst file (12 bad / 25).
- **A second fabricated-comparative cluster lives in the PBR docs.** `PBR_D_VALIDATION_REPORT` / `PBR_D_EXECUTIVE_SUMMARY` / `PBR_F_DESIGN` assert "competitive with UE5 (~150-200 ALU)", "parity with AAA engines", and per-device frame-rate targets (Mali-G78 45 FPS / PS5 90 FPS / RTX 3070 120 FPS) with no benchmark behind them — the same invented-competitor-number pattern D.0 found in the journey archive, here in present-tense reference docs.
- **The phantom cargo aliases recur in five more files.** `check-all` / `build-core` / `test-all` / `clippy-all` are documented as working in `.github/CI_README.md`, `CLAUDE_MD_HARDENING_PROPOSAL`, `QWEN3_MIGRATION_PLAN`, `WHAT_DIDNT`, and `BENCHMARKING_PHILOSOPHY` — only `editor*` aliases exist in `.cargo/config.toml`. CODE-FINDING-adjacent: the docs describe a tooling surface that was never created.
- **`docs/reference/Interfaces.md` documents a `WorldSnapshot` that does not exist** (fields `version/tick/time_ms/self_id/rng_seed/region` vs the real `t/player/me/enemies/pois/obstacles/objective`), plus `EntityView`/`HealthView`/`ObjectiveHint`/`HazardHint` types absent from the code — a `28bc94f21`-class invented-API reference page, FABRICATED.
- **90 ⚠️CONTRADICTION rows** — the new tag. Dominated by the render plans (103k stated as both "current Strength" and "Before:" baseline within one file) and the security plan (`sign16` finding present-tense while the code already moved to HMAC). These route to D.1 as reconcile-or-collapse, not single-value patches.

### 6.2 Rewrite-beats-patch (locked decision: delete hallucinated content; rewrite only where a real fact exists to document faithfully)

**Delete-dominant (mostly fabricated/hallucinated — excise, do not patch):**
- `docs/reference/Interfaces.md` — documents a non-existent `WorldSnapshot`/`EntityView`/`HealthView`/`MaterialGraph` API surface (FABRICATED). Replace with a generated-from-code reference or delete.
- The competitor-comparison blocks in `RENDERER_DEEP_ANALYSIS_AND_MEGALIGHTS_PLAN.md`, `RENDERER_MASTER_IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md`, `COMPREHENSIVE_AUDIT_REPORT.md`, `COMPETITIVE_ANALYSIS_SUMMARY.md`, `EXTERNAL_RESEARCH_COMPETITIVE_ANALYSIS.md` — delete the invented `10.4× / 2.1-5.2× / 103k` rows (keep any genuinely externally-cited competitor figure).
- The PBR "competitive with UE5 / parity with AAA / per-device FPS targets" claims in `PBR_D_VALIDATION_REPORT`, `PBR_D_EXECUTIVE_SUMMARY`, `PBR_F_DESIGN`, `PBR_F_COMPLETION_SUMMARY` — delete (no benchmark exists).
- The `check-all`/`build-core`/`test-all`/`clippy-all` alias instructions in `.github/CI_README.md`, `CLAUDE_MD_HARDENING_PROPOSAL.md`, `QWEN3_MIGRATION_PLAN.md`, `WHAT_DIDNT.md` — delete or replace with the real `editor*` aliases + explicit per-crate commands.
**Rewrite (real fact exists, framing is wrong):**
- `astraweave-fluids/README.md` — SPH/caustics/foam are real in-crate; rewrite to research-surface / zero-production-consumer framing (not "production capability").
- `CLAUDE_MD_HARDENING_PROPOSAL.md` — it quotes a stale CLAUDE.md (128 crates / 3,892 editor tests); rewrite the quoted block to current ground truth or mark it explicitly as a historical quotation.

## 7. Honest limits

1. **Coverage is complete for the 386-file set: 0 unswept.** All 386 appear in the manifest with a line count and `readFully:true`. 150 yielded zero present-tense claims (historical narration) — that is the expected shape, not a gap.
2. **One path variant.** The misc-historical agent reported `docs/terrain-research/README.md`; the manifest path is `docs/reference/terrain-research/README.md`. Both resolve to the same terrain-research README content; treated as covered. No claims either way.
3. **3 historical-batch groups initially hit the session limit** (`tools-editor-historical`, `tools-assets-historical`, `misc-historical`) and were re-run via workflow resume; the final merge includes all 29 groups. No file in those groups is unswept.
4. **All C1 perf, coverage %, Miri/Kani counts are UNVERIFIABLE-IN-SWEEP by policy** (412 rows). D.0.1 ran no benchmarks/tests/coverage/Miri. Each carries its D.2 reproduction command. Cost must not silently upgrade these to VERIFIED.
5. **Present-tense vs historical is a judgment call** on plan/report docs that mix a current-state preamble with forward roadmap. The rule applied: a claim is in scope only if a reader today would take it as a statement of the engine's *current* capability/status/metric. Borderline plan-aspiration was tagged ASPIRATIONAL-AS-PRESENT rather than dropped, erring toward inventorying.
6. **Security CODE-FINDINGs are doc-sourced, spot-verified.** The SECURITY plan's still-true findings (plaintext WebSocket, prompt logging, sandbox) were grep-confirmed at the cited lines this sweep but not exhaustively audited; they route to the security campaign for full confirmation, not fixed here.

*D.0.1 inventoried 873 present-tense claims across the 386-file gap set (29 groups + 1 gap-closer), closing the reachability gap D.0 named. Merged with D.0: 2137 total classified claims across the full 524-file in-scope corpus. Read-only; `git status` clean except this report. Next: **D.1** prose corrections + `CLAIMS_REGISTRY.md` migration, gated on Andrew's review of the merged D.0 + D.0.1 inventory.*
